***хан.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хан.html>хан</a> (5031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mongolic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Mongolic languages">Mongolic</a></span> source, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mongolian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Mongolian language">Mongolian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mn"><a href = vnd.unilang:кан.html>хаан</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">haan</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from the same <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кага́н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kagán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>A possible intermediary is <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chagatai_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chagatai language">Chagatai</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="chg">خان</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="chg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xan</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хан.html>хан</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xan</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хан.html>ха́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хан.html>ха́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хан.html>ха́нов</a></b>)
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hypochondria</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὑποχόνδρια</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hupokhóndria</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хандра.html>хандра́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xandrá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хандра.html>хандры́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ханжа.html>ханжа́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xanžá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ество</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-estvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***хапать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хапать.html>ха́пать</a> (29497)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xāpàti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хапать.html>ха́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xápatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сха́пать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ха́пнуть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rude</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to grab (quickly); to steal; to take (from someone unlawfully)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rude</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take bribes</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:характеризоваться.html>характеризова́ться</a> (8968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:характерный.html>Характерно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>них</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проголосовать.html>проголосова́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:против.html>про́тив</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>



</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:характерный.html>характерный</a> (2880)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:характерный.html>характе́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xaraktérnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)характе́рнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)характе́рней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>possessing pronounced, distinctive features</li>
<li>characteristic, particular, typical, specific</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:характерный.html>характе́рно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xaraktérno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">характе́рность</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xaraktérnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:характер.html>хара́ктер</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xarákter</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:характерный.html>хара́ктерный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xarákternyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)хара́ктернее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)хара́ктерней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> theater</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> character <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">expressing a certain psychological type</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:характерный.html>хара́ктерный</a></b> актёр</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>xarákternyj</b> aktjór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">character actor</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> strong-willed, having a strong character</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>харч</a> (11961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">харчь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xarčĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">خَرْج</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ḵarj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">expenditure, outlay, expense, costs</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, via a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> language: compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">harç</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Azerbaijani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Azerbaijani language">Azerbaijani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="az">xərc</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>харч</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xarč</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:харч.html>ха́рча</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:харч.html>харчи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:харч.html>харче́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> grub, food
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебирать.html>перебира́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:харч.html>харча́ми</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">perebirátʹ <b>xarčámi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be overly picky (<i>also figuratively</i>)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>харч</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">metátʹ <b>xarč</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to vomit</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:харя.html>ха́ря</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xárja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:харя.html>ха́ри</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:харя.html>ха́ри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:харя.html>харь</a></b>)

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:хата.html>ха́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xáta</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house; home</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хата.html>ха́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xáta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хата.html>ха́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хата.html>ха́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хата.html>хат</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(a peasant's) house, hut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойдём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хата.html>ха́ту</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pojdjóm v <b>xátu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">let's go inside</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">let's go into the house</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> house, joint, a place one can booze or have sex
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вчера.html>вчера́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>буха́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> ко́реша <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хата.html>ха́те</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">včerá my buxáli u kóreša na <b>xáte</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">yesterday/last night we boozed at pal's place (note: preposition "<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a>" is used in this sense)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukraine" class="extiw" title="w:Ukraine">Ukraine</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Russia" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Russia">Southern Russia</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> home
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хата.html>ха́та</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:край.html>кра́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mojá <b>xáta</b> s kráju, ja ničevó ne znáju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">none of my business</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">my home is on the edge (of the village), I don't know anything</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> prison cell</li></ol>

***хаять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хаять.html>ха́ять</a> (13532)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хаять.html>ха́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xájatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оха́ять</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slander, to backbite, to slag off, to find fault (with), to run down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:хаять.html>ха́ют</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спино́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ют</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ангел.html>а́нгел</a>... <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хотя́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подрезать.html>подре́зать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>кры́лья</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jésli tebjá <b>xájut</b> za tvojéj spinój, oní prósto znájut, što ty ángel... i xotját podrézatʹ tebé krýlʹja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">If they slander you behind your back, they simply know that you're an angel... and want to cut your wings.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***хвала.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвала.html>хвала́</a> (15232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвала.html>хвала́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xvala</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*xvala</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвала.html>хвала́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">xvalá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвала.html>хвалы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвала.html>хвалы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural missing</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>praise, glory</li></ol>
